# PA вҶ” vPA delta-log (flogence вҖ” scrmlTS adaptation)

**Ratified S199 (2026-06-16); deputy-reframed S203 (2026-06-17).** The fine-grained PAвҶ’deputy absorption
stream. The deputy (the persistent vPA вҖ” `vpa-scrml.md`) reads `[last-absorbed+1 .. now]` on a poke to
stay current WITHOUT re-reading the fat hand-off or cold-reading the docs. Append-only. Migrates into the
`flogence` repo when it's built; lives here now for the 2-manual-terminal immediate-benefit mode.

**Format:** one block per entry вҖ”
```
[seq] kind  В· what-happened  В· вҶ’ pointer  В· (vpa: directive)
```
- **kind** вҲҲ `rule` (user decision) В· `disp` (agent fired) В· `land` (commit landed) В· `find` (gap/bug/finding) В· `state` (board/test/sync delta) В· ~~`baton` (handoff)~~ (RETIRED S202 вҖ” deputy model; historical entries S199 [17][18] / S200 [8][9] only). A deputy reboot-gap entry (Function 3, LIVE S203) is an ordinary `state` entry flagged `(deputy)`.
- **pointer** = SHA / file:line / gap-id / doc / agent-id (the vPA pulls detail only if needed)
- **(vpa: вҖҰ)** = optional; the ONLY field that asks the vPA to do/note something (hold В· sandbox a debate В· take ownership of agent X В· absorb-and-stand-by). Most entries omit it.
- **trailing tags (post-S199, flogence-graph era):** `@to:<files>` (read-set вҖ” what was touched) В· `@as:<disposition>` (`landed`/`ratified`/`resolved`/`minted`/вҖҰ) В· `@r:<render-set>` (**INFERRED** вҖ” kind+targetsвҶ’renders; flogence-derived, PA may omit) В· **`@adv:<thread-id>[,<id>]`** (**AUTHORED** вҖ” which reasoning-thread(s) this delta materially ADVANCES; the cross-grade graph edge `@to` [a file read-set] structurally can't carry; the id is a flograph node / `@gap id=`; optional + back-compat, untagged = no edge) В· `#xref:<proj>[:thread]` (cross-PA reference). **The boundary (RATIFIED S230; flogence co-adopt):** *author the JUDGMENT (`@adv` / `@as`), infer the MECHANICS (`@r`).* `@adv` is the judgment axis `@to`/`@as` left uncovered.

**Cadence:** the PA appends an entry at the moments it would write a hand-off bullet вҖ” a ruling, a
dispatch, a landing, a finding, a state delta вҖ” NOT per tool-call. The vPA absorbs the batch
since-last-poke at sparse checkpoints (prompt-cache TTL вҶ’ don't poke constantly; keep vPA context lean).

**Relationship to the other logs:** distinct from user-voice (verbatim user statements, durable) and
the changelog (per-session landings, coarse). This is the live PA-state stream the deputy absorbs; it does NOT
replace the wrap hand-off (kept for cold-start safety + audit) вҖ” it replaces the deputy's *dependence* on it.

**Single-writer rule (refined S203):** only the LIVE PA appends to the source stream. The deputy is read-only
on this file вҖ” the one narrow exception is the Function-3 (LIVE S203) reboot-gap entry (an ordinary `state` entry
flagged `(deputy)`, observation-only, recording an agent that landed while the PA was rebooting; never substantive).
